posted:Posted December 5, 2023
msg:The day of check-in was Saturday night. The door of the hotel was relatively hidden and no one guided us. The door could not be found. The air conditioner was extremely hot that night. I set the maximum wind speed to 16 degrees, and the indoor temperature was still 25-26 degrees. However, I was given a thick quilt and was woken up by the heat and could not fall asleep. It was still hot at about 10 pm the next night. I called the front desk, and the front desk said that the general engineering depar**ent had turned off the main switch of the air conditioner because the weather was getting cooler. I asked if it could be turned on. The front desk communicated with the engineering depar**ent later before it was turned on. At this point, things were already very strange. After all, it is a five-star hotel. I think the temperature of the air-conditioned room should be adjusted by myself, and this hotel is not central air-conditioned. However, because they had helped solve the problem, I did not express dissatisfaction with the fact that I could not sleep due to the heat the night before. I only mentioned that I could not sleep due to the heat the night before when communicating with the front desk. Then on the third day, I was woken up by the heat at around 1 am, and the indoor temperature It was 25 degrees. When I woke up, it was 26 degrees. It was only after I called the front desk that the temperature dropped to 25 degrees. When I woke up in the morning, the indoor temperature was still 25 degrees. The 16-degree air conditioner was useless. The hotel asked about changing rooms at 2 a.m., but it was really troublesome to change rooms in the middle of the night, and I didn't dare to let the waiter come in at midnight. But after I called later, the room temperature did start to drop, so I just slept. Then the most speechless thing began. The hotel said the next day that the air conditioner couldn't be turned down because there were three people in the room. I was looking at the suite, not the smallest double room. In the end, I thought that the air conditioner couldn't be turned down to below 20 degrees for three people in the room, which meant that there was something wrong with the air conditioner. The hotel kept shirking the responsibility by saying that there were too many people, and that no one had ever said that the hotel air conditioner was hot, but the next room was still cold. That was even more ridiculous. I'm not the manager of the hotel. I should know whether the next room was cold or hot? In the end, I looked through the negative reviews and found that there were also people saying it was hot. It seems that the hotel's ventilation system is indeed problematic.
I didn't want to give 1 star at first, but I gave 1 star to the little robot that delivered the food, and 1 star to the waiter who cleaned our room the next day, wrote a small note, and gave us laundry detergent and disposable hangers.
In addition, during the dispute on the last day, the hotel staff said that the coffee was not free, because I asked if I could drink it for free on the first day and the other party said that I had just drunk it. It was also wrong to drink coffee during the dispute. Anyway, it was quite speechless.
The good impression that Fuzhou, the city, gave me was ruined by this hotel. It's really unlucky! People who live here should think carefully.
All the disputes were recorded and videotaped, and the final compensation was also inconsistent. They felt that we were blackmailed. I don't know how to complain to the hotel in the most useful way. I hope that later visitors can give me a channel to complain.
